            if (verticalOpenPct < 20) {
              open.classList.add('tight');
            }

            const fill = document.createElement('div');
            fill.className = 'manual-schematic-stack-fill';
            fill.style.height = `${Math.max(verticalFillPct, 4)}%`;

            body.appendChild(open);
            body.appendChild(fill);

            const length = document.createElement('div');
            length.className = 'manual-schematic-stack-length';
            length.textContent = `${displayLength.toFixed(1)} ft`;

            stack.appendChild(body);
            stack.appendChild(length);
            track.appendChild(stack);
          });

          if (remainingFt > 0.05) {
            const remainingWidthPct = Math.max((remainingFt / widthBase) * 100, 8);
            const empty = document.createElement('div');
            empty.className = 'manual-schematic-stack is-remaining';
            empty.style.width = `${remainingWidthPct}%`;
            empty.innerHTML = `
              <div class="manual-schematic-stack-body empty">
                <div class="manual-schematic-empty-text">${remainingFt.toFixed(1)} ft remaining</div>
                <div class="manual-schematic-empty-sub">MAX HEIGHT: 13'6"</div>
              </div>
              <div class="manual-schematic-stack-length">${remainingFt.toFixed(1)} ft</div>
            `;
            track.appendChild(empty);
          }

          host.appendChild(track);
          const foot = document.createElement('div');
          foot.className = 'manual-schematic-deck-foot';
          foot.textContent = `${formatFeet(deckLength)} deck length`;
          host.appendChild(foot);
          return host;
        };

        const upperDeckLength = toFeet(schematic.upper_deck_length);
        const lowerDeckLength = toFeet(schematic.lower_deck_length);
        if (upperDeckLength > 0.02) {
          const stepDeckRow = document.createElement('div');
          stepDeckRow.className = 'manual-schematic-stepdeck-row';
          const lowerDeckCap = lowerDeckLength > 0.02
            ? lowerDeckLength
            : Math.max(capacity - upperDeckLength, 1);

          const upperDeck = buildDeck(
            'Upper Deck',
            upperDeckLength,
            toFeet(schematic.upper_remaining_ft),
            decks.upper || [],
          );
          upperDeck.style.flex = `${Math.max(upperDeckLength, 1)} 1 0`;

          const lowerDeck = buildDeck(
            'Lower Deck',
            lowerDeckCap,
            toFeet(schematic.lower_remaining_ft),
            decks.lower || [],
          );
          lowerDeck.style.flex = `${Math.max(lowerDeckCap, 1)} 1 0`;

          stepDeckRow.appendChild(upperDeck);
          stepDeckRow.appendChild(lowerDeck);
          capacityVisual.appendChild(stepDeckRow);
        } else {
          capacityVisual.appendChild(
            buildDeck(
              'Lower Deck',
              lowerDeckLength || capacity,
              toFeet(schematic.lower_remaining_ft),
              decks.lower || [],
            ),
          );
        }

        const overflowByOrder = {};
        let remainingWithin = Math.max(capacity - baseWithin, 0);
        selectedList.forEach((order) => {
          const orderFt = toFeet(order.total_length_ft);
          if (orderFt <= 0.02) return;
          const withinFt = Math.min(orderFt, remainingWithin);
          const overflowFt = Math.max(orderFt - withinFt, 0);
          if (overflowFt > 0.02) {
            overflowByOrder[order.so_num] = overflowFt;
          }
          remainingWithin = Math.max(remainingWithin - withinFt, 0);
        });

        const selectedStrip = document.createElement('div');
        selectedStrip.className = 'manual-add-selected-strip';
        if (!selectedList.length) {
          const none = document.createElement('div');
          none.className = 'subtext';
          none.textContent = 'Select suggested orders to preview how remaining feet are consumed.';
          selectedStrip.appendChild(none);
        } else {
          selectedList.forEach((order) => {
            const chip = document.createElement('span');
            chip.className = 'manual-add-selected-chip';
            chip.style.setProperty('--chip-accent', orderColor(order.so_num));
            const extra = overflowByOrder[order.so_num] ? ` (${formatFeet(overflowByOrder[order.so_num])} over)` : '';
            if (overflowByOrder[order.so_num]) chip.classList.add('is-over');
            chip.textContent = `#${order.so_num} +${formatFeet(order.total_length_ft)}${extra}`;
            selectedStrip.appendChild(chip);
          });
        }
        capacityVisual.appendChild(selectedStrip);

        if (overByProjected > 0.05) {
          const overflowHint = document.createElement('div');
          overflowHint.className = 'manual-add-capacity-overflow';
          overflowHint.textContent = `Projected overflow: ${formatFeet(overByProjected)} beyond available deck length`;
          capacityVisual.appendChild(overflowHint);
        }

        if (capacitySummary) {
          const baseText = `Current ${formatFeet(baseUsed)} | Selected +${formatFeet(selectedTotal)} | Projected ${formatFeet(projectedUsed)}`;
          if (overByProjected > 0.05) {
            capacitySummary.textContent = `${baseText} | Over by ${formatFeet(overByProjected)}`;
            capacitySummary.classList.add('is-over');
          } else {
            capacitySummary.textContent = `${baseText} | ${formatFeet(remainingProjected)} remaining`;
            capacitySummary.classList.remove('is-over');
          }
        }
      };

      const evaluateFitState = (order, soNum) => {
        const capacity = toFeet(cachedSpace.capacity_ft);
        if (!capacity) {
          return { className: 'unknown', text: 'Capacity Unknown' };
        }
        const baseUsed = toFeet(cachedSpace.used_ft);
        const orderFt = toFeet(order.total_length_ft);
        const currentlySelected = getSelectedTotalFt();
        const alreadySelected = selectedOrders.has(soNum);
        const projected = baseUsed + currentlySelected + (alreadySelected ? 0 : orderFt);
        const overBy = Math.max(projected - capacity, 0);
        if (overBy > 0.05) {
          return { className: 'over', text: `Over Capacity by ${overBy.toFixed(1)} ft` };
        }
        return { className: 'ok', text: 'Within Capacity' };
      };

      const closeModal = () => {
        if (isSubmitting) return;
        if (activeController) activeController.abort();
        activeController = null;
        activeLoadId = null;
        cachedSuggestions = [];
        cachedSpace = {};
        cachedExistingSchematic = null;
        selectedOrders = new Map();
        searchTerm = '';
        setSubmittingState(false);
        closeProgressModal();
        setError('');
        if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
        if (meta) meta.textContent = '';
        if (utilMeta) utilMeta.textContent = '';
        renderCapacityPlaceholder('Existing SKU footprint and remaining feet will appear here.');
        modal.classList.add('hidden');
      };

      const updateSubmitState = () => {
        if (!submitBtn) return;
        submitBtn.disabled = isSubmitting || selectedOrders.size === 0;
      };

      const renderEmpty = (message) => {
        if (!list) return;
        list.innerHTML = '';
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'subtext';
        div.textContent = message;
        list.appendChild(div);
      };

      const updateUtilizationUI = () => {
        renderCapacityVisual();
      };

      const renderSuggestionList = () => {
        if (!list) return;
        list.innerHTML = '';

        const query = (searchTerm || '').trim().toLowerCase();
        const visible = cachedSuggestions.filter((item) => {
          const soNum = (item.so_num || '').toString().trim();
          if (!soNum) return false;
          if (!query) return true;
          const skuTerms = (Array.isArray(item.sku_breakdown) ? item.sku_breakdown : [])
            .map((entry) => (entry.sku || '').toString())
            .join(' ');
          const haystack = [
            soNum,
            item.cust_name || '',
            item.due_date || '',
            item.city || '',
            item.state || '',
            item.zip || '',
            skuTerms,
          ]
            .join(' ')
            .toLowerCase();
          return haystack.includes(query);
        });

        if (meta) {
          const selectedCount = selectedOrders.size;
          meta.textContent = `${visible.length} shown of ${cachedSuggestions.length} available | ${selectedCount} selected (+${getSelectedTotalFt().toFixed(1)} ft)`;
        }

        if (!visible.length) {
          renderEmpty(query ? 'No orders match your search.' : 'No draft-scope orders are available to add.');
          updateSubmitState();
          updateUtilizationUI();
          return;
        }

        visible.forEach((item) => {
          const soNum = (item.so_num || '').toString().trim();
          if (!soNum) return;

          const row = document.createElement('label');
          row.className = 'manual-order-item checkbox';

          const checkbox = document.createElement('input');
          checkbox.type = 'checkbox';
          checkbox.name = 'so_nums';
          checkbox.value = soNum;
          checkbox.checked = selectedOrders.has(soNum);
          checkbox.addEventListener('change', () => {
            const normalized = normalizeOrder(item);
            if (checkbox.checked) {
              selectedOrders.set(soNum, normalized);
            } else {
              selectedOrders.delete(soNum);
            }
            renderSuggestionList();
          });

          const textWrap = document.createElement('div');
          textWrap.className = 'manual-order-text';

          const title = document.createElement('div');
          title.className = 'manual-order-title';
          const titleBits = [`#${soNum}`];
          if (item.distance_miles != null) titleBits.push(`${item.distance_miles} mi`);
          if (item.stack_added_ft != null) titleBits.push(`+${Number(item.stack_added_ft || item.total_length_ft || 0).toFixed(1)} stack ft`);
          title.textContent = titleBits.join(' | ');

          const metaRow = document.createElement('div');
          metaRow.className = 'manual-order-meta';
          const cust = (item.cust_name || '').toString().trim();
          const due = (item.due_date || '').toString().trim();
          const city = (item.city || '').toString().trim();
          const state = (item.state || '').toString().trim();
          const metaBitsRow = [
            cust || 'Customer',
            due ? `Due ${due}` : 'Due --',
            `${city || ''}${city && state ? ', ' : ''}${state || ''}`.trim(),
          ].filter(Boolean);
          if (item.utilization_pct != null) metaBitsRow.push(`${Math.round(item.utilization_pct || 0)}% util`);
          metaRow.textContent = metaBitsRow.join(' | ');

          const fitState = evaluateFitState(item, soNum);
          const fitRow = document.createElement('div');
          fitRow.className = 'manual-order-fit-row';
          const fitBadge = document.createElement('span');
          fitBadge.className = `manual-fit-badge ${fitState.className}`;
          fitBadge.textContent = fitState.text;
          fitRow.appendChild(fitBadge);

          const skuRow = document.createElement('div');
          skuRow.className = 'manual-order-skus';
          const skuEntries = normalizeSkuBreakdown(item.sku_breakdown);
          if (skuEntries.length) {
            skuEntries.slice(0, 5).forEach((entry) => {
              const chip = document.createElement('span');
              chip.className = 'manual-sku-chip';
              chip.textContent = `${entry.sku} ${formatFeet(entry.ft)}`;
              skuRow.appendChild(chip);
            });
            if (skuEntries.length > 5) {
              const overflowChip = document.createElement('span');
              overflowChip.className = 'manual-sku-chip manual-sku-chip-overflow';
              overflowChip.textContent = `+${skuEntries.length - 5} more`;
              skuRow.appendChild(overflowChip);
            }
          } else {
            const emptyChip = document.createElement('span');
            emptyChip.className = 'manual-sku-chip manual-sku-chip-empty';
            emptyChip.textContent = 'No SKU detail';
            skuRow.appendChild(emptyChip);
          }

          textWrap.appendChild(title);
          textWrap.appendChild(metaRow);
          textWrap.appendChild(fitRow);
          textWrap.appendChild(skuRow);

          row.appendChild(checkbox);
          row.appendChild(textWrap);
          list.appendChild(row);
        });

        updateSubmitState();
        updateUtilizationUI();
      };

      const renderSuggestions = (payload) => {
        cachedSuggestions = Array.isArray(payload.suggestions) ? payload.suggestions.map((order) => normalizeOrder(order)) : [];
        cachedSpace = payload.space || {};
        cachedExistingSchematic = payload.existing_schematic || null;
        selectedOrders = new Map();
        updateSubmitState();
        updateUtilizationUI();
        renderSuggestionList();
      };

      const loadSuggestions = (loadId) => {
        if (!list) return;
        cachedSuggestions = [];
        cachedSpace = {};
        cachedExistingSchematic = null;
        selectedOrders = new Map();
        updateSubmitState();
        setError('');
        if (meta) meta.textContent = '';
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="subtext">Loading suggestions...</div>';
        if (submitBtn) submitBtn.disabled = true;
        if (utilMeta) utilMeta.textContent = '';
        renderCapacityPlaceholder('Loading existing SKU footprint and remaining feet...');

        if (activeController) activeController.abort();
        activeController = new AbortController();

        fetch(`/loads/${loadId}/manual_add/suggestions`, { signal: activeController.signal })
          .then((response) => response.json().then((data) => ({ ok: response.ok, data })))
          .then(({ ok, data }) => {
            if (!ok) {
              throw new Error((data && data.error) || 'Suggestion lookup failed.');
            }
            renderSuggestions(data || {});
          })
          .catch((err) => {
            if (err && err.name === 'AbortError') return;
            renderEmpty('Suggestion lookup failed. Try again.');
            renderCapacityPlaceholder('Suggestion lookup failed. Try again.');
          });
      };

      const startReoptPolling = (statusUrl, redirectUrl) => {
        const url = (statusUrl || '').trim();
        if (!url) {
          window.location.assign(redirectUrl || window.location.href);
          return;
        }

        const startedAt = Date.now();
        let attempts = 0;
        const maxAttempts = 400;
        const pollIntervalMs = 3000;
        const renderElapsed = () => {
          const elapsedSec = Math.max(Math.floor((Date.now() - startedAt) / 1000), 0);
          const mm = String(Math.floor(elapsedSec / 60)).padStart(2, '0');
          const ss = String(elapsedSec % 60).padStart(2, '0');
          if (progressMeta) progressMeta.textContent = `Please wait... ${mm}:${ss} elapsed`;
        };
        renderElapsed();
        if (elapsedTimer) {
          window.clearInterval(elapsedTimer);
          elapsedTimer = null;
        }
        elapsedTimer = window.setInterval(renderElapsed, 1000);

        const poll = () => {
          fetch(url)
            .then((response) => response.json().then((payload) => ({ ok: response.ok, payload })))
            .then(({ ok, payload }) => {
              if (!ok) {
                throw new Error((payload && payload.error) || 'Unable to check re-optimization status.');
              }
              const status = (payload && payload.status ? payload.status : '').toLowerCase();
              if (status === 'running') {
                attempts += 1;
                if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                  const timeoutError = new Error('Re-optimization is taking longer than expected. Refresh to check status.');
                  timeoutError.isTerminal = true;
                  throw timeoutError;
                }
                pollTimer = window.setTimeout(poll, pollIntervalMs);
                return;
              }
              if (status === 'done') {
                if (elapsedTimer) {
                  window.clearInterval(elapsedTimer);
                  elapsedTimer = null;
                }
                window.location.assign(redirectUrl || window.location.href);
                return;
              }
              const failedMessage = (payload && payload.error) || 'Re-optimization failed. Please try again.';
              const terminalError = new Error(failedMessage);
              terminalError.isTerminal = true;
              throw terminalError;
            })
            .catch((err) => {
              if (err && err.isTerminal) {
                closeProgressModal();
                setSubmittingState(false);
                setError(err.message || 'Re-optimization failed. Please try again.');
                return;
              }
              attempts += 1;
              if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                closeProgressModal();
                setSubmittingState(false);
                setError('Re-optimization is taking longer than expected. Refresh to check status.');
                return;
              }
              pollTimer = window.setTimeout(poll, pollIntervalMs);
            });
        };

        poll();
      };

      const openModal = (loadId) => {
        activeLoadId = loadId;
        setSubmittingState(false);
        closeProgressModal();
        setError('');
        modal.classList.remove('hidden');
        searchTerm = '';
        if (searchInput) {
          searchInput.value = '';
        }
        loadSuggestions(loadId);
      };

      manualAddApi = { open: openModal, close: closeModal };

      if (closeButton) closeButton.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
      if (cancelButton) cancelButton.addEventListener('click', closeModal);

      modal.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        if (event.target === modal) {
          closeModal();
        }
      });

      document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
        if (event.key !== 'Escape') return;
        if (modal.classList.contains('hidden')) return;
        closeModal();
      });

      if (form) {
        form.addEventListener('submit', (event) => {
          event.preventDefault();
          if (isSubmitting) return;
          setError('');
          if (!activeLoadId) return;

          const selected = Array.from(selectedOrders.keys());
          if (!selected.length) return;

          const confirmMsg = 'Convert this load to MANUAL, add the selected orders, and re-optimize remaining orders?';
          if (!window.confirm(confirmMsg)) return;

          setSubmittingState(true);
          openProgressModal('Applying manual updates and re-optimizing remaining orders...');
          const formData = new FormData();
          selected.forEach((soNum) => formData.append('so_nums', soNum));

          fetch(`/loads/${activeLoadId}/manual_add`, { method: 'POST', body: formData })
            .then((response) => response.json().then((data) => ({ ok: response.ok, data })))
            .then(({ ok, data }) => {
              if (!ok) {
                throw new Error((data && data.error) || 'Unable to add orders.');
              }
              const statusUrl = (data && data.status_url) || '';
              const redirectUrl = (data && data.redirect_url) || window.location.href;
              startReoptPolling(statusUrl, redirectUrl);
            })
            .catch((err) => {
              closeProgressModal();
              setSubmittingState(false);
              setError((err && err.message) || 'Unable to add orders. Try again.');
              updateSubmitState();
            });
        });
      }

      if (searchInput) {
        searchInput.addEventListener('input', () => {
          searchTerm = searchInput.value || '';
          renderSuggestionList();
        });
      }
    }

    function initLoadsPlantCards() {
      const container = document.querySelector('.loads-plant-cards');
      if (!container) return;
      const storageKey = 'loads-last-plants';
      container.querySelectorAll('[data-plant]').forEach((card) => {
        card.addEventListener('click', () => {
          const plant = (card.dataset.plant || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          if (!plant) return;

          const url = new URL(window.location.href);
          const params = url.searchParams;
          const currentPlantsParam = (params.get('plants') || '').trim().toUpperCase();
          const isAllMode = !currentPlantsParam || currentPlantsParam === 'ALL';

          if (plant === 'ALL') {
            if (isAllMode) {
              const last = (window.localStorage.getItem(storageKey) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
              if (last && last !== 'ALL') {
                params.set('plants', last);
              } else {
                params.delete('plants');
              }
            } else {
              window.localStorage.setItem(storageKey, currentPlantsParam);
              params.delete('plants');
            }
          } else {
            const selected = new Set(
              (params.get('plants') || '')
                .split(',')
                .map((value) => value.trim().toUpperCase())
                .filter(Boolean)
            );

            if (isAllMode) selected.clear();

            if (selected.has(plant)) {
              selected.delete(plant);
            } else {
              selected.add(plant);
            }

            if (!selected.size) {
              params.delete('plants');
              window.localStorage.removeItem(storageKey);
            } else {
              const next = Array.from(selected).join(',');
              params.set('plants', next);
              window.localStorage.setItem(storageKey, next);
            }
          }

          url.search = params.toString();
          window.location.assign(url.toString());
        });
      });
    }

    function bindSchematicEditButtons(root = document) {
      root.querySelectorAll('.js-schematic-edit-open').forEach((btn) => {
        if (btn.dataset.bound === 'true') return;
        btn.dataset.bound = 'true';
        btn.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
          event.preventDefault();
          event.stopPropagation();
          const loadId = btn.dataset.loadId;
          if (!loadId) return;
          if (!schematicEditApi || typeof schematicEditApi.open !== 'function') return;
          schematicEditApi.open(loadId);
        });
      });
    }

    function initSchematicEditModal() {
      const modal = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-modal');
      if (!modal) return;

      const closeButton = modal.querySelector('[data-schematic-edit-close]');
      const cancelButton = modal.querySelector('[data-schematic-edit-cancel]');
      const resetButton = modal.querySelector('[data-schematic-edit-reset]');
      const saveButton = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-save');
      const subtitle = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-subtitle');
      const metricsHost = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-metrics');
      const canvas = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-canvas');
      const warningHost = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-warning-list');
      const errorHost = document.getElementById('schematic-edit-error');

      const state = {
        loadId: null,
        trailerType: 'STEP_DECK',
        units: [],
        unitsById: {},
        layout: { positions: [] },
        originalLayout: { positions: [] },
        baseLayout: { positions: [] },
        warnings: [],
        metrics: {},
        assumptions: {
          stack_overflow_max_height: 5,
          max_back_overhang_ft: 4,
          upper_two_across_max_length_ft: 7,
          upper_deck_exception_max_length_ft: 16,
          upper_deck_exception_overhang_allowance_ft: 6,
          upper_deck_exception_categories: ['USA', 'UTA'],
        },
        draggingUnitId: null,
      };

      const cloneLayout = (layout) => JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(layout || { positions: [] }));

      const setError = (message) => {
        if (!errorHost) return;
        if (!message) {
          errorHost.classList.add('hidden');
          errorHost.textContent = '';
          return;
        }
        errorHost.textContent = message;
        errorHost.classList.remove('hidden');
      };

      const trailerProfiles = {{ trailer_profile_options | tojson }};
      const trailerConfig = (trailerType) => {
        const key = String(trailerType || 'STEP_DECK').trim().toUpperCase();
        const profile = (trailerProfiles || []).find((entry) => String(entry.value || '').toUpperCase() === key);
        if (profile) {
          return {
            lower: Number(profile.lower || 0),
            upper: Number(profile.upper || 0),
            capacity: Number(profile.capacity || 0),
          };
        }
        return { lower: 53, upper: 0, capacity: 53 };
      };

      const findPosition = (positionId) => (
        (state.layout.positions || []).find((pos) => (pos.position_id || '') === (positionId || ''))
      );

      const removeUnitFromLayout = (unitId) => {
        let removed = false;
        state.layout.positions = (state.layout.positions || [])
          .map((pos) => {
            const nextIds = (pos.unit_ids || []).filter((id) => id !== unitId);
            if (nextIds.length !== (pos.unit_ids || []).length) {
              removed = true;
            }
            return { ...pos, unit_ids: nextIds };
          })
          .filter((pos) => (pos.unit_ids || []).length > 0 || !!pos.allow_empty);
        return removed;
      };

      const ensurePositionIds = () => {
        state.layout.positions = (state.layout.positions || []).map((pos, idx) => ({
          ...pos,
          position_id: pos.position_id || `p${idx + 1}`,
        }));
      };

      const insertUnitInPosition = (unitId, positionId, index) => {
        const pos = findPosition(positionId);
        if (!pos) return;
        const list = pos.unit_ids || [];
        const targetIndex = Math.max(0, Math.min(Number(index || 0), list.length));
        list.splice(targetIndex, 0, unitId);
        pos.unit_ids = list;
        if (pos.allow_empty) pos.allow_empty = false;
      };

      const moveUnitToPosition = (unitId, positionId, index) => {
        if (!unitId || !positionId) return;
        removeUnitFromLayout(unitId);
        insertUnitInPosition(unitId, positionId, index);
        ensurePositionIds();
        computeClientPreview();
        render();
      };

      const moveUnitToNewStack = (unitId, deck, insertIndex) => {
        if (!unitId) return;
        removeUnitFromLayout(unitId);
        const targetDeck = (deck || 'lower') === 'upper' ? 'upper' : 'lower';
        const newPos = { position_id: `p${Date.now()}`, deck: targetDeck, unit_ids: [unitId] };
        const positions = state.layout.positions || [];
        const deckPositions = positions.filter((pos) => (pos.deck || 'lower') === targetDeck);
        if (!deckPositions.length) {
          state.layout.positions.push(newPos);
        } else {
          const deckIndices = positions
            .map((pos, idx) => ({ pos, idx }))
            .filter((entry) => (entry.pos.deck || 'lower') === targetDeck)
            .map((entry) => entry.idx);
          const boundedInsert = Math.max(0, Math.min(Number(insertIndex || 0), deckIndices.length));
          const insertAt =
            boundedInsert >= deckIndices.length
              ? (deckIndices[deckIndices.length - 1] + 1)
              : deckIndices[boundedInsert];
          positions.splice(insertAt, 0, newPos);
          state.layout.positions = positions;
        }
        ensurePositionIds();
        computeClientPreview();
        render();
      };

      const createEmptyStack = (deck, insertIndex) => {
        const targetDeck = (deck || 'lower') === 'upper' ? 'upper' : 'lower';
        const newPos = {
          position_id: `p${Date.now()}-${Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000)}`,
          deck: targetDeck,
          unit_ids: [],
          allow_empty: true,
        };
        const positions = state.layout.positions || [];
        const deckPositions = positions.filter((pos) => (pos.deck || 'lower') === targetDeck);
        if (!deckPositions.length) {
          positions.push(newPos);
          state.layout.positions = positions;
        } else {
          const deckIndices = positions
            .map((pos, idx) => ({ pos, idx }))
            .filter((entry) => (entry.pos.deck || 'lower') === targetDeck)
            .map((entry) => entry.idx);
          const boundedInsert = Math.max(0, Math.min(Number(insertIndex || 0), deckIndices.length));
          const insertAt =
            boundedInsert >= deckIndices.length
              ? (deckIndices[deckIndices.length - 1] + 1)
              : deckIndices[boundedInsert];
          positions.splice(insertAt, 0, newPos);
          state.layout.positions = positions;
        }
        ensurePositionIds();
        computeClientPreview();
        render();
      };

      const renderWarnings = () => {
        if (!warningHost) return;
        warningHost.innerHTML = '';
        const warnings = state.warnings || [];
        if (!warnings.length) {
          const empty = document.createElement('div');
          empty.className = 'subtext';
          empty.textContent = 'No warnings.';
          warningHost.appendChild(empty);
          return;
        }
        warnings.forEach((warning) => {
          const row = document.createElement('div');
          row.className = 'schematic-edit-warning-item';
          row.textContent = warning.message || warning.code || 'Warning';
          warningHost.appendChild(row);
        });
      };

      const renderMetrics = () => {
        if (!metricsHost) return;
        const metrics = state.metrics || {};
        const util = Number(metrics.utilization_pct || 0);
        const grade = metrics.utilization_grade || 'F';
        const linear = Number(metrics.total_linear_feet || 0).toFixed(1);
        metricsHost.innerHTML = [
          `<span><strong>Utilization:</strong> ${util.toFixed(1)}%</span>`,
          `<span><strong>Grade:</strong> ${grade}</span>`,
          `<span><strong>Length:</strong> ${linear} ft</span>`,
          `<span><strong>Warnings:</strong> ${(state.warnings || []).length}</span>`,
        ].join('');
      };

      const computeClientPreview = () => {
        const cfg = trailerConfig(state.trailerType);
        const assumptions = state.assumptions || {};
        const stackOverflowMaxHeight = Math.max(
          Number(assumptions.stack_overflow_max_height || 0),
          0,
        );
        const maxBackOverhangFt = Math.max(
          Number(assumptions.max_back_overhang_ft || 0),
          0,
        );
        const upperTwoAcrossMaxLengthFt = Math.max(
          Number(assumptions.upper_two_across_max_length_ft || 0),
          0,
        );
        const upperDeckExceptionMaxLengthFt = Math.max(
          Number(assumptions.upper_deck_exception_max_length_ft || 0),
          0,
        );
        const upperDeckExceptionOverhangAllowanceFt = Math.max(
          Number(assumptions.upper_deck_exception_overhang_allowance_ft || 0),
          0,
        );
        const normalizeExceptionCategories = (value) => {
          const source = Array.isArray(value)
            ? value
            : (typeof value === 'string' ? value.split(',') : []);
          const cleaned = [];
          const seen = new Set();
          source.forEach((entry) => {
            const normalized = String(entry || '').trim().toUpperCase();
            if (!normalized || seen.has(normalized)) return;
            seen.add(normalized);
            cleaned.push(normalized);
          });
          return cleaned.length ? cleaned : ['USA', 'UTA'];
        };
        const upperDeckExceptionCategories = normalizeExceptionCategories(
          assumptions.upper_deck_exception_categories
        );
        const upperDeckExceptionCategorySet = new Set(upperDeckExceptionCategories);
        const trailerKey = String(state.trailerType || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        const isStepDeckProfile = trailerKey.startsWith('STEP_DECK');
        const maxStackUtilizationMultiplier = stackOverflowMaxHeight > 0
          ? (1 + (1 / stackOverflowMaxHeight))
          : 1;
        const warnings = [];
        let lowerTotal = 0;
        let upperTotal = 0;
        let eligibleUpperTotal = 0;
        let totalLinear = 0;
        let credit = 0;
        const unitFraction = (maxStack) => 1 / Math.max(Number(maxStack || 1), 1);
        const allowsSingleOverflow = (units, capUsed) => {
          if (!(capUsed > 1.000001)) return false;
          if (!(stackOverflowMaxHeight > 0)) return false;
          if (capUsed > (maxStackUtilizationMultiplier + 0.000001)) return false;
          return (units || []).some((unit, unitIdx) => {
            const maxStack = Math.max(Number(unit.max_stack || 1), 1);
            if (maxStack < stackOverflowMaxHeight) return false;
            if ((capUsed - unitFraction(maxStack)) > 1.000001) return false;
            const baseHeights = new Set(
              (units || [])
                .filter((_, baseIdx) => baseIdx !== unitIdx)
                .map((baseUnit) => Math.max(Number(baseUnit.max_stack || 1), 1))
            );
            return baseHeights.size >= 2;
          });
        };

        (state.layout.positions || []).forEach((pos, idx) => {
          const ids = pos.unit_ids || [];
          const units = ids.map((id) => state.unitsById[id]).filter(Boolean);
          if (!units.length) return;
          const deck = (pos.deck || 'lower') === 'upper' ? 'upper' : 'lower';
          const categories = units
            .map((unit) => String(unit.category || '').trim().toUpperCase())
            .filter(Boolean);
          const hasOnlyEligibleCategories = categories.length > 0
            && categories.every((category) => upperDeckExceptionCategorySet.has(category));
          const unitsForCapacity = units.map((unit) => {
            const effectiveMax = Math.max(
              Number(
                (isStepDeckProfile && deck === 'upper')
                  ? (unit.upper_max_stack || unit.max_stack || 1)
                  : (unit.max_stack || 1)
              ),
              1,
            );
            return { ...unit, max_stack: effectiveMax };
          });
          const length = Math.max(...units.map((unit) => Number(unit.unit_length_ft || 0)));
          const capUsed = unitsForCapacity.reduce((sum, unit) => {
            const maxStack = Math.max(Number(unit.max_stack || 1), 1);
            return sum + (1 / maxStack);
          }, 0);
          const overflowApplied = allowsSingleOverflow(unitsForCapacity, capUsed);
          let overflowNote = '';
          const requiredUpperStacks = deck === 'upper'
            ? Math.max(Math.ceil(Math.max(capUsed - 0.000001, 0)), 1)
            : 1;
          const twoAcrossEligible = (
            isStepDeckProfile
            && deck === 'upper'
            && upperTwoAcrossMaxLengthFt > 0
            && length <= (upperTwoAcrossMaxLengthFt + 0.000001)
          );
          const effectiveLength = deck === 'upper'
            ? (
              twoAcrossEligible
                ? (Math.ceil(requiredUpperStacks / 2) * length)
                : (requiredUpperStacks * length)
            )
            : length;
          const upperLengthLimit = (
            isStepDeckProfile
            && deck === 'upper'
            && hasOnlyEligibleCategories
          )
            ? Math.max(cfg.upper, upperDeckExceptionMaxLengthFt)
            : cfg.upper;
          const exceptionEligibleUpperPosition = (
            isStepDeckProfile
            && deck === 'upper'
            && hasOnlyEligibleCategories
            && length > (cfg.upper + 0.000001)
            && length <= (upperLengthLimit + 0.000001)
          );

          totalLinear += effectiveLength;
          credit += effectiveLength * (overflowApplied
            ? Math.min(capUsed, maxStackUtilizationMultiplier)
            : Math.min(capUsed, 1));
          if (deck === 'upper') {
            upperTotal += effectiveLength;
            if (exceptionEligibleUpperPosition) {
              eligibleUpperTotal += effectiveLength;
            }
            if (cfg.upper > 0) {
              const tooLong = units.some(
                (unit) => Number(unit.unit_length_ft || 0) > (upperLengthLimit + 0.000001)
              );
              if (tooLong) {
                warnings.push({
                  code: 'ITEM_TOO_BIG_FOR_UPPER_DECK',
                  message: `Position ${idx + 1}: one or more items exceed ${upperLengthLimit.toFixed(1)} ft upper deck limit.`,
                });
              }
            }
          } else {
            lowerTotal += length;
          }

          pos.upper_required_stack_count = requiredUpperStacks;
          pos.upper_two_across_eligible = !!twoAcrossEligible;
          pos.two_across_applied = !!(twoAcrossEligible && requiredUpperStacks >= 2);
          pos.two_across_note = pos.two_across_applied
            ? `items less than ${upperTwoAcrossMaxLengthFt.toFixed(1).replace(/\.0$/, '')} ft stacked 2 across to allow for additional capacity`
            : '';
          pos.effective_length_ft = effectiveLength;

          if (capUsed > (maxStackUtilizationMultiplier + 0.000001)) {
            warnings.push({
              code: 'STACK_TOO_HIGH',
              message: `Position ${idx + 1}: stack fill is ${capUsed.toFixed(2)}x, above allowed ${maxStackUtilizationMultiplier.toFixed(2)}x.`,
            });
          } else if (capUsed > 1.000001) {
            if (overflowApplied) {
              overflowNote = `Stack ${idx + 1} was overutilized to allow for additional space (${capUsed.toFixed(2)}x, allowed up to ${maxStackUtilizationMultiplier.toFixed(2)}x).`;
              warnings.push({
                code: 'STACK_OVERFLOW_ALLOWANCE_USED',
                message: overflowNote,
              });
            } else {
              warnings.push({
                code: 'STACK_TOO_HIGH',
                message: `Position ${idx + 1}: stack fill is ${capUsed.toFixed(2)}x and is not eligible for overflow allowance.`,
              });
            }
          }
          pos.overflow_applied = !!overflowApplied;
          pos.overflow_note = overflowNote;

          const lengths = units.map((unit) => Number(unit.unit_length_ft || 0));
          for (let i = 1; i < lengths.length; i += 1) {
            if (lengths[i] > lengths[i - 1] + 0.0001) {
              warnings.push({
                code: 'COMPATIBILITY_ISSUE',
                message: `Position ${idx + 1}: invalid stack (longer item above shorter item).`,
              });
              break;
            }
          }

          if (categories.includes('DUMP') && new Set(categories).size > 1) {
            warnings.push({
              code: 'COMPATIBILITY_ISSUE',
              message: `Position ${idx + 1}: DUMP items cannot mix with other categories.`,
            });
          }
        });

        const lowerOverhang = Math.max(lowerTotal - cfg.lower, 0);
        if (lowerOverhang > 0.05) {
          warnings.push({
            code: lowerOverhang <= (maxBackOverhangFt + 0.000001)
              ? 'BACK_OVERHANG_IN_ALLOWANCE'
              : 'ITEM_HANGS_OVER_DECK',
            message: lowerOverhang <= (maxBackOverhangFt + 0.000001)
              ? `Lower deck back overhang is ${lowerOverhang.toFixed(1)} ft (allowance ${maxBackOverhangFt.toFixed(1)} ft).`
              : `Lower deck back overhang is ${lowerOverhang.toFixed(1)} ft, exceeding allowance by ${(lowerOverhang - maxBackOverhangFt).toFixed(1)} ft.`,
          });
        }
        const upperOverhang = Math.max(upperTotal - cfg.upper, 0);
        const upperExceptionExtraCap = Math.max(
          upperDeckExceptionOverhangAllowanceFt - maxBackOverhangFt,
          0,
        );
        const eligibleOverhangPotential = Math.max(eligibleUpperTotal - cfg.upper, 0);
        const eligibleExtraAllowance = Math.min(eligibleOverhangPotential, upperExceptionExtraCap);
        const upperAllowedOverhang = maxBackOverhangFt + eligibleExtraAllowance;
        if (cfg.upper > 0 && upperOverhang > 0.05) {
          warnings.push({
            code: upperOverhang <= (upperAllowedOverhang + 0.000001)
              ? 'BACK_OVERHANG_IN_ALLOWANCE'
              : 'ITEM_HANGS_OVER_DECK',
            message: upperOverhang <= (upperAllowedOverhang + 0.000001)
              ? `Upper deck back overhang is ${upperOverhang.toFixed(1)} ft (allowance ${upperAllowedOverhang.toFixed(1)} ft).`
              : `Upper deck back overhang is ${upperOverhang.toFixed(1)} ft, exceeding allowance by ${(upperOverhang - upperAllowedOverhang).toFixed(1)} ft.`,
          });
        }

        const utilizationPct = cfg.capacity > 0 ? ((credit / cfg.capacity) * 100) : 0;
        const grade = utilizationPct >= 85
          ? 'A'
          : utilizationPct >= 70
            ? 'B'
            : utilizationPct >= 55
              ? 'C'
              : utilizationPct >= 40
                ? 'D'
                : 'F';

        state.warnings = warnings;
        state.metrics = {
          utilization_pct: utilizationPct,
          utilization_grade: grade,
          total_linear_feet: totalLinear,
          utilization_credit_ft: credit,
          exceeds_capacity: cfg.upper > 0
            ? (
              lowerTotal > (cfg.lower + maxBackOverhangFt)
              || upperTotal > (cfg.upper + upperAllowedOverhang)
            )
            : (totalLinear > (cfg.lower + maxBackOverhangFt)),
        };
      };

      const getPositionLengthFt = (position) => {
        const ids = (position && position.unit_ids) || [];
        const lengths = ids
          .map((id) => state.unitsById[id])
          .filter(Boolean)
          .map((unit) => Number(unit.unit_length_ft || 0));
        return lengths.length ? Math.max(...lengths) : 0;
      };

      const getDeckUsageFt = (deckKey) => (
        (state.layout.positions || [])
          .filter((pos) => (pos.deck || 'lower') === deckKey)
          .reduce((sum, pos) => {
            if (deckKey === 'upper') {
              return sum + Number(pos.effective_length_ft || getPositionLengthFt(pos) || 0);
            }
            return sum + getPositionLengthFt(pos);
          }, 0)
      );

      const twoAcrossGroupKey = (unit) => {
        if (!unit) return '';
        const stopSequence = Number(unit.stop_sequence);
        if (Number.isFinite(stopSequence)) return `stop:${stopSequence}`;
        const orderId = String(unit.order_id || '').trim();
        if (orderId) return `order:${orderId}`;
        const sku = String(unit.sku || '').trim();
        if (sku) return `sku:${sku}`;
        return 'misc';
      };

      const buildTwoAcrossColumns = (ids) => {
        const groups = [];
        (ids || []).forEach((unitId) => {
          const unit = state.unitsById[unitId];
          if (!unit) return;
          const key = twoAcrossGroupKey(unit);
          const last = groups[groups.length - 1];
          if (last && last.key === key) {
            last.ids.push(unitId);
          } else {
            groups.push({ key, ids: [unitId] });
          }
        });

        const totalUnits = groups.reduce((sum, group) => sum + group.ids.length, 0);
        const leftTarget = Math.floor(totalUnits / 2);
        const rightTarget = totalUnits - leftTarget;
        let leftRemaining = leftTarget;
        let rightRemaining = rightTarget;
        const preferredSideByGroup = new Map();
        const leftIds = [];
        const rightIds = [];

        groups.forEach((group) => {
          const count = group.ids.length;
          if (!count) return;

          let preferredSide = preferredSideByGroup.get(group.key);
          if (preferredSide !== 'left' && preferredSide !== 'right') {
            preferredSide = rightRemaining >= leftRemaining ? 'right' : 'left';
          }
          let secondarySide = preferredSide === 'right' ? 'left' : 'right';

          let preferredRemaining = preferredSide === 'right' ? rightRemaining : leftRemaining;
          let secondaryRemaining = preferredSide === 'right' ? leftRemaining : rightRemaining;

          let preferredCount = 0;
          let secondaryCount = 0;
          if (count <= preferredRemaining) {
            preferredCount = count;
          } else if (count <= secondaryRemaining) {
            preferredSide = secondarySide;
            secondarySide = preferredSide === 'right' ? 'left' : 'right';
            preferredRemaining = preferredSide === 'right' ? rightRemaining : leftRemaining;
            secondaryRemaining = preferredSide === 'right' ? leftRemaining : rightRemaining;
            preferredCount = count;
          } else {
            preferredCount = Math.min(count, preferredRemaining);
            secondaryCount = count - preferredCount;
            if (secondaryCount > secondaryRemaining) {
              const overflow = secondaryCount - secondaryRemaining;
              secondaryCount = secondaryRemaining;
              preferredCount += overflow;
            }
          }

          let leftCount = preferredSide === 'left' ? preferredCount : secondaryCount;
          let rightCount = preferredSide === 'right' ? preferredCount : secondaryCount;

          leftCount = Math.max(Math.min(leftCount, leftRemaining), 0);
          rightCount = Math.max(Math.min(rightCount, rightRemaining), 0);
          let assigned = leftCount + rightCount;
          if (assigned < count) {
            let deficit = count - assigned;
            const rightSpace = Math.max(rightRemaining - rightCount, 0);
            const leftSpace = Math.max(leftRemaining - leftCount, 0);
            if (rightSpace >= leftSpace && rightSpace > 0) {
              const add = Math.min(deficit, rightSpace);
              rightCount += add;
              deficit -= add;
            }
            if (deficit > 0 && leftSpace > 0) {
              leftCount += Math.min(deficit, leftSpace);
            }
          }

          const rightSlice = group.ids.slice(0, rightCount);
          const leftSlice = group.ids.slice(rightCount, rightCount + leftCount);
          rightIds.push(...rightSlice);
          leftIds.push(...leftSlice);

          leftRemaining -= leftCount;
          rightRemaining -= rightCount;
          preferredSideByGroup.set(group.key, rightCount >= leftCount ? 'right' : 'left');
        });

        return { leftIds, rightIds };
      };

      const renderDeck = (deckKey, options = {}) => {
        const showUpperVoid = !!options.showUpperVoid;
        const stackIndexByPositionId = options.stackIndexByPositionId || {};
        const wrapper = document.createElement('div');
        wrapper.className = 'schematic-edit-deck';
        wrapper.dataset.deck = deckKey;
        wrapper.classList.add(deckKey === 'upper' ? 'is-upper' : 'is-lower');

        const cfg = trailerConfig(state.trailerType);
        const deckCap = deckKey === 'upper' ? cfg.upper : cfg.lower;
        const title = document.createElement('div');
        title.className = 'schematic-edit-deck-title';
        title.textContent = `${deckKey === 'upper' ? 'Upper' : 'Lower'} Deck (${deckCap.toFixed(1)} ft)`;
        wrapper.appendChild(title);

        const stage = document.createElement('div');
        stage.className = 'schematic-edit-deck-stage';
        wrapper.appendChild(stage);

        const track = document.createElement('div');
        track.className = 'schematic-edit-deck-track';
        if (showUpperVoid) {
          track.classList.add('has-unavailable-zone');
        }
        stage.appendChild(track);

        if (showUpperVoid) {
          const unavailable = document.createElement('div');
          unavailable.className = 'schematic-edit-upper-void';
          unavailable.innerHTML = '<span class="schematic-edit-upper-void-label">Unavailable</span>';
          stage.appendChild(unavailable);
        }

        const positions = (state.layout.positions || [])
          .filter((pos) => (pos.deck || 'lower') === deckKey);
        const allowLeftInsertSlots = true;

        const createStackSlot = (insertIdx) => {
          const slot = document.createElement('div');
          slot.className = 'schematic-edit-stack-slot';
          slot.dataset.deck = deckKey;
          slot.dataset.insertIndex = String(insertIdx);
          slot.textContent = '+';
          slot.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Create new stack');
          slot.title = 'Click to create an empty stack or drag a unit here.';
          slot.addEventListener('click', () => {
            createEmptyStack(deckKey, insertIdx);
          });
          slot.addEventListener('dragover', (event) => {
            event.preventDefault();
            slot.classList.add('dragover');
          });
          slot.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
            slot.classList.remove('dragover');
          });
          slot.addEventListener('drop', (event) => {
            event.preventDefault();
            slot.classList.remove('dragover');
            const unitId = state.draggingUnitId || event.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
            if (!unitId) return;
            moveUnitToNewStack(unitId, deckKey, insertIdx);
          });
          return slot;
        };

        const appendDeckUsage = () => {
          const deckUsageFt = getDeckUsageFt(deckKey);
          const usage = document.createElement('div');
          usage.className = 'schematic-edit-deck-usage';
          usage.innerHTML = `
            <div class="schematic-edit-deck-usage-line" aria-hidden="true"></div>
            <div class="schematic-edit-deck-usage-value${deckUsageFt > deckCap + 0.05 ? ' is-over' : ''}">
              ${deckUsageFt.toFixed(1)} / ${deckCap.toFixed(1)} ft used
            </div>
          `;
          wrapper.appendChild(usage);
        };

        if (!positions.length) {
          track.appendChild(createStackSlot(0));
          appendDeckUsage();
          return wrapper;
        }

        positions.forEach((pos, posIdx) => {
          if (allowLeftInsertSlots) {
            track.appendChild(createStackSlot(posIdx));
          }

          const stackCol = document.createElement('div');
          stackCol.className = 'schematic-edit-stack';
          stackCol.dataset.positionId = pos.position_id;
          const isTwoAcross = deckKey === 'upper' && !!pos.two_across_applied;
          if (isTwoAcross) stackCol.classList.add('is-two-across');

          const positionLengthFt = getPositionLengthFt(pos);
          stackCol.style.setProperty('--position-length-ft', String(positionLengthFt || 0));
          stackCol.style.flex = `${Math.max(positionLengthFt || 1, 1)} 1 0`;

          const stackHeader = document.createElement('div');
          stackHeader.className = 'schematic-edit-stack-header';
          const stackLabelNumber = Number(stackIndexByPositionId[pos.position_id] || (posIdx + 1));
          stackHeader.innerHTML = `
            <span>Stack ${stackLabelNumber}</span>
            <span class="schematic-edit-stack-length">${Number(positionLengthFt || 0).toFixed(1)} ft</span>
          `;
          stackCol.appendChild(stackHeader);

          const stackBody = document.createElement('div');
          stackBody.className = 'schematic-edit-stack-body';
          stackBody.addEventListener('dragover', (event) => {
            event.preventDefault();
          });
          stackBody.addEventListener('drop', (event) => {
            event.preventDefault();
            const unitId = state.draggingUnitId || event.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
            if (!unitId) return;
            moveUnitToPosition(unitId, pos.position_id, (pos.unit_ids || []).length);
          });
          stackCol.appendChild(stackBody);

          const ids = pos.unit_ids || [];
          const createDropSlot = (targetIndex) => {
            const drop = document.createElement('div');
            drop.className = 'schematic-edit-drop-slot';
            drop.dataset.positionId = pos.position_id;
            drop.dataset.index = String(targetIndex);
            drop.addEventListener('dragover', (event) => {
              event.preventDefault();
              drop.classList.add('dragover');
            });
            drop.addEventListener('dragleave', () => {
              drop.classList.remove('dragover');
            });
            drop.addEventListener('drop', (event) => {
              event.preventDefault();
              event.stopPropagation();
              drop.classList.remove('dragover');
              const unitId = state.draggingUnitId || event.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
              if (!unitId) return;
              moveUnitToPosition(unitId, pos.position_id, targetIndex);
            });
            return drop;
          };

          const createUnitElement = (unitId) => {
            const unit = state.unitsById[unitId];
            if (!unit) return null;
            const unitEl = document.createElement('div');
            unitEl.className = 'schematic-edit-unit';
            unitEl.draggable = true;
            unitEl.dataset.unitId = unitId;
            unitEl.style.setProperty('--unit-accent', unit.color || '#137fec');
            const unitLengthFt = Number(unit.unit_length_ft || 0);
            const ratioRaw = positionLengthFt > 0 ? (unitLengthFt / positionLengthFt) : 1;
            const ratio = Math.max(0.24, Math.min(1, ratioRaw || 1));
            unitEl.style.setProperty('--unit-length-ratio', String(ratio));
            unitEl.innerHTML = `
              <div class="schematic-edit-unit-main">${unit.item || unit.sku || 'UNIT'}</div>
              <div class="schematic-edit-unit-meta">${Number(unitLengthFt || 0).toFixed(1)} ft</div>
            `;
            unitEl.addEventListener('dragstart', (event) => {
              state.draggingUnitId = unitId;
              event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
              event.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', unitId);
              unitEl.classList.add('dragging');
            });
            unitEl.addEventListener('dragend', () => {
              state.draggingUnitId = null;
              unitEl.classList.remove('dragging');
            });
            return unitEl;
          };

          if (!isTwoAcross) {
            stackBody.appendChild(createDropSlot(0));
            ids.forEach((unitId, idx) => {
              const unitEl = createUnitElement(unitId);
              if (!unitEl) return;
              stackBody.appendChild(unitEl);
              stackBody.appendChild(createDropSlot(idx + 1));
            });
          } else {
            const { leftIds, rightIds } = buildTwoAcrossColumns(ids);
            const leftColumn = document.createElement('div');
            leftColumn.className = 'schematic-edit-two-across-column left';
            const rightColumn = document.createElement('div');
            rightColumn.className = 'schematic-edit-two-across-column right';

            leftIds.forEach((unitId) => {
              const unitEl = createUnitElement(unitId);
              if (unitEl) leftColumn.appendChild(unitEl);
            });
            rightIds.forEach((unitId) => {
              const unitEl = createUnitElement(unitId);
              if (unitEl) rightColumn.appendChild(unitEl);
            });

            stackBody.appendChild(leftColumn);
            stackBody.appendChild(rightColumn);

            const marker = document.createElement('span');
            marker.className = 'schematic-edit-stack-two-across-icon material-symbols-outlined';
            marker.textContent = 'view_week';
            const thresholdFt = Number((state.assumptions || {}).upper_two_across_max_length_ft || 7);
            const thresholdLabel = Number.isFinite(thresholdFt)
              ? thresholdFt.toFixed(1).replace(/\.0$/, '')
              : '7';
            marker.dataset.tooltip = `items less than ${thresholdLabel} ft stacked 2 across to allow for additional capacity`;
            stackBody.appendChild(marker);
          }

          track.appendChild(stackCol);
        });

        track.appendChild(createStackSlot(positions.length));
        appendDeckUsage();
        return wrapper;
      };

      const render = () => {
        if (subtitle) {
          subtitle.textContent = state.loadId
            ? `Load ${state.loadId} | ${String(state.trailerType || '').replace('_', ' ')}`
            : 'Drag units between stacks and decks, then save.';
        }
        renderWarnings();
        renderMetrics();
        if (!canvas) return;
        canvas.innerHTML = '';
        const cfg = trailerConfig(state.trailerType);
        const orderedPositions = Array.isArray(state.layout.positions) ? state.layout.positions : [];
        const stackIndexByPositionId = {};
        orderedPositions.forEach((pos, idx) => {
          if (pos && pos.position_id) stackIndexByPositionId[pos.position_id] = idx + 1;
        });
        const lowerDeck = renderDeck('lower', { stackIndexByPositionId });
        if (cfg.upper > 0) {
          const stepDeckRow = document.createElement('div');
          stepDeckRow.className = 'schematic-edit-stepdeck-row';
          const totalDeckFt = Math.max(Number(cfg.lower || 0) + Number(cfg.upper || 0), 1);
          const lowerPct = (Math.max(Number(cfg.lower || 1), 1) / totalDeckFt) * 100;
          const upperPct = (Math.max(Number(cfg.upper || 1), 1) / totalDeckFt) * 100;
          lowerDeck.style.flex = `0 0 ${lowerPct}%`;
          const upperDeck = renderDeck('upper', { showUpperVoid: true, stackIndexByPositionId });
          upperDeck.style.flex = `0 0 ${upperPct}%`;
          stepDeckRow.appendChild(lowerDeck);
          stepDeckRow.appendChild(upperDeck);
          canvas.appendChild(stepDeckRow);
          return;
        }
        canvas.appendChild(lowerDeck);
      };

      const closeModal = () => {
        state.loadId = null;
        state.units = [];
        state.unitsById = {};
        state.layout = { positions: [] };
        state.originalLayout = { positions: [] };
        state.baseLayout = { positions: [] };
        state.warnings = [];
        state.metrics = {};
        state.assumptions = {
          stack_overflow_max_height: 5,
          max_back_overhang_ft: 4,
          upper_two_across_max_length_ft: 7,
          upper_deck_exception_max_length_ft: 16,
          upper_deck_exception_overhang_allowance_ft: 6,
          upper_deck_exception_categories: ['USA', 'UTA'],
        };
        state.draggingUnitId = null;
        setError('');
        if (canvas) canvas.innerHTML = '<div class="subtext">Loading schematic editor...</div>';
        if (warningHost) warningHost.innerHTML = '<div class="subtext">No warnings.</div>';
        if (metricsHost) metricsHost.innerHTML = '';
        modal.classList.add('hidden');
      };

      const parseJsonPayload = async (response) => {
        const contentType = (response.headers.get('content-type') || '').toLowerCase();
        if (contentType.includes('application/json')) {
          try {
            return await response.json();
          } catch (_error) {
            return null;
          }
        }
        const text = await response.text();
        if (!text) return null;
        try {
          return JSON.parse(text);
        } catch (_error) {
          return null;
        }
      };

      const openModal = (loadId) => {
        setError('');
        state.loadId = String(loadId);
        modal.classList.remove('hidden');
        if (canvas) canvas.innerHTML = '<div class="subtext">Loading schematic editor...</div>';
        fetch(`/loads/${encodeURIComponent(loadId)}/schematic/edit`)
          .then(async (response) => ({ ok: response.ok, payload: await parseJsonPayload(response) }))
          .then(({ ok, payload }) => {
            if (!ok) {
              throw new Error(
                (payload && payload.error) ||
                (payload && payload.redirect_url ? 'Session expired. Please sign in again.' : '') ||
                'Unable to open schematic editor.'
              );
            }
            if (!payload.can_edit) {
              throw new Error('Approved loads are read-only.');
            }
            state.trailerType = payload.trailer_type || 'STEP_DECK';
            state.units = Array.isArray(payload.units) ? payload.units : [];
            state.unitsById = {};
            state.units.forEach((unit) => {
              if (unit && unit.unit_id) state.unitsById[unit.unit_id] = unit;
            });
            state.layout = cloneLayout(payload.layout);
            state.originalLayout = cloneLayout(payload.layout);
            state.baseLayout = cloneLayout(payload.base_layout || payload.layout);
            state.assumptions = {
              stack_overflow_max_height: 5,
              max_back_overhang_ft: 4,
              upper_two_across_max_length_ft: 7,
              upper_deck_exception_max_length_ft: 16,
              upper_deck_exception_overhang_allowance_ft: 6,
              upper_deck_exception_categories: ['USA', 'UTA'],
              ...(payload.assumptions || {}),
            };
            computeClientPreview();
            render();
          })
          .catch((error) => {
            setError((error && error.message) || 'Unable to open schematic editor.');
            if (canvas) canvas.innerHTML = '<div class="subtext">Unable to load editor.</div>';
          });
      };

      const saveLayout = (confirmViolation = false) => {
        if (!state.loadId) return Promise.reject(new Error('No load selected.'));
        return fetch(`/loads/${encodeURIComponent(state.loadId)}/schematic/edit/save?tab=${encodeURIComponent(loadsTab || '')}`, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            trailer_type: state.trailerType,
            layout: state.layout,
            confirm_violation: confirmViolation,
            tab: loadsTab || '',
          }),
        }).then(async (response) => ({ response, payload: await parseJsonPayload(response) }));
      };

      if (saveButton) {
        saveButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
          setError('');
          saveButton.disabled = true;
          saveLayout(false)
            .then(({ response, payload }) => {
              if (response.status === 409 && payload && payload.requires_confirmation) {
                const warningLines = (payload.warnings || [])
                  .slice(0, 6)
                  .map((warning) => `- ${warning.message}`)
                  .join('\n');
                const confirmed = window.confirm(
                  `Saving will keep warnings on this schematic.\n${warningLines || '- Warnings detected.'}\n\nContinue?`
                );
                if (!confirmed) {
                  throw new Error('Save canceled');
                }
                return saveLayout(true);
              }
              if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error((payload && payload.error) || 'Unable to save schematic.');
              }
              return { response, payload };
            })
            .then(({ response, payload }) => {
              if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error((payload && payload.error) || 'Unable to save schematic.');
              }
              if (!state.loadId) return null;
              return fetchSchematic(state.loadId, { force: true });
            })
            .then(() => {
              closeModal();
            })
            .catch((error) => {
              if (error && error.message === 'Save canceled') return;
              setError((error && error.message) || 'Unable to save schematic.');
            })
            .finally(() => {
              saveButton.disabled = false;
            });
        });
      }

      if (resetButton) {
        resetButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
          state.layout = cloneLayout(state.baseLayout || state.originalLayout);
          computeClientPreview();
          render();
        });
      }
      if (closeButton) closeButton.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
      if (cancelButton) cancelButton.addEventListener('click', closeModal);

      modal.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
        if (event.target === modal) closeModal();
      });

      document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
        if (event.key !== 'Escape') return;
        if (modal.classList.contains('hidden')) return;
        closeModal();
      });

      schematicEditApi = { open: openModal, close: closeModal };
    }

    function initSessionStopwatch() {
      const tooltips = document.querySelectorAll('[data-session-tooltip]');
      if (!tooltips.length) return;

      const formatDuration = (ms) => {
        const totalSeconds = Math.max(Math.floor(ms / 1000), 0);
        const hours = String(Math.floor(totalSeconds / 3600)).padStart(2, '0');
        const minutes = String(Math.floor((totalSeconds % 3600) / 60)).padStart(2, '0');
        const seconds = String(totalSeconds % 60).padStart(2, '0');
        return `${hours}:${minutes}:${seconds}`;
      };

      tooltips.forEach((tooltip) => {
        const startRaw = tooltip.dataset.startTs || '';
        const archivedRaw = tooltip.dataset.archivedTs || '';
        const display = tooltip.querySelector('[data-session-stopwatch]');
        if (!display || !startRaw) return;

        const startTime = new Date(startRaw);
        if (archivedRaw) {
          const endTime = new Date(archivedRaw);
          display.textContent = formatDuration(endTime - startTime);
          return;
        }

        const tick = () => {
          display.textContent = formatDuration(Date.now() - startTime.getTime());
        };
        tick();
        setInterval(tick, 1000);
      });
    }

    function initReoptStatusPolling() {
      const reoptStatus = {{ (reopt_status or '') | tojson }};
      const reoptJobId = {{ (reopt_job_id or '') | tojson }};
      if (reoptStatus !== 'running' || !reoptJobId) return;

      const buildStatusUrl = () => `/loads/reopt_jobs/${encodeURIComponent(reoptJobId)}`;
      const buildRedirectUrl = (status) => {
        const next = new URL(window.location.href);
        next.searchParams.set('reopt', status);
        next.searchParams.delete('reopt_job');
        return next.toString();
      };

      let attempts = 0;
      const maxAttempts = 120; // 6 minutes at 3s polling
      const pollIntervalMs = 3000;

      const poll = () => {
        fetch(buildStatusUrl())
          .then((response) => response.json().then((payload) => ({ ok: response.ok, payload })))
          .then(({ ok, payload }) => {
            if (!ok) {
              throw new Error((payload && payload.error) || 'Status check failed.');
            }

            const status = (payload && payload.status ? payload.status : '').toLowerCase();
            if (status === 'running') {
              attempts += 1;
              if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
                window.location.replace(buildRedirectUrl('failed'));
                return;
              }
              window.setTimeout(poll, pollIntervalMs);
              return;
            }

            if (status === 'done') {
              window.location.replace(buildRedirectUrl('done'));
              return;
            }

            window.location.replace(buildRedirectUrl('failed'));
          })
          .catch(() => {
            attempts += 1;
            if (attempts >= maxAttempts) {
              window.location.replace(buildRedirectUrl('failed'));
              return;
            }
            window.setTimeout(poll, pollIntervalMs);
          });
      };

      window.setTimeout(poll, 1200);
    }

    initFreightBreakdownModal();
    initManualLoadModal();
    initManualAddModal();
    initSchematicEditModal();
    initLoadsPlantCards();
    bindManualAddButtons();
    bindSchematicEditButtons();
    initReoptStatusPolling();
    initSessionStopwatch();

    function initSchematicHoverTooltips() {
      if (window.__schematicHoverTooltipsBound) return;
      window.__schematicHoverTooltipsBound = true;

      const tooltip = document.createElement('div');
      tooltip.className = 'schematic-hover-tooltip hidden';
      tooltip.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      document.body.appendChild(tooltip);

      let activeTarget = null;

      const escapeTooltipHtml = (value) => String(value || '')
        .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
        .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
        .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
        .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');

      function formatTooltipHtml(text) {
        const rawParts = String(text || '')
          .split('|')
          .map((part) => part.trim())
          .filter(Boolean);
        if (!rawParts.length) return '';

        // SKU unit tooltips are structured with pipe-delimited key/value fragments.
        // We drop redundant first line, remove stop, and merge Length + Max stack.
        const isSkuUnitTooltip = rawParts.some((part) => /^SKU\s*:/i.test(part));
        if (!isSkuUnitTooltip) {
          return rawParts
            .map((part) => `<div class="schematic-hover-tooltip-row">${escapeTooltipHtml(part)}</div>`)
            .join('');
        }

        const parts = rawParts.slice(1); // remove first line (item label), redundant with visible SKU label
        const nonStop = parts.filter((part) => !/^Stop\s*:/i.test(part));
        const lengthPart = nonStop.find((part) => /^Length\s*:/i.test(part));
        const maxStackPart = nonStop.find((part) => /^Max stack\s*:/i.test(part));
        const core = nonStop.filter(
          (part) => !/^Length\s*:/i.test(part) && !/^Max stack\s*:/i.test(part)
        );
        if (lengthPart || maxStackPart) {
          core.push([lengthPart, maxStackPart].filter(Boolean).join(' | '));
        }
        return core
          .map((part) => `<div class="schematic-hover-tooltip-row">${escapeTooltipHtml(part)}</div>`)
          .join('');
      }

      function positionTooltip(evt) {
        if (!activeTarget) return;
        const pad = 14;
        const rect = tooltip.getBoundingClientRect();
        let left = evt.clientX + pad;
        let top = evt.clientY + pad;
        if (left + rect.width > window.innerWidth - 10) left = Math.max(10, evt.clientX - rect.width - pad);
        if (top + rect.height > window.innerHeight - 10) top = Math.max(10, evt.clientY - rect.height - pad);
        tooltip.style.left = `${left}px`;
        tooltip.style.top = `${top}px`;
      }

      function hideTooltip() {
        activeTarget = null;
        tooltip.classList.add('hidden');
        tooltip.innerHTML = '';
      }

      document.addEventListener('mouseover', (evt) => {
        const target = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('[data-tooltip]') : null;
        if (!target) return;
        const text = target.getAttribute('data-tooltip');
        if (!text) return;
        activeTarget = target;
        tooltip.innerHTML = formatTooltipHtml(text);
        tooltip.classList.remove('hidden');
      });

      document.addEventListener('mousemove', (evt) => {
        if (!activeTarget) return;
        positionTooltip(evt);
      });

      document.addEventListener('mouseout', (evt) => {
        if (!activeTarget) return;
        const leaving = evt.target && evt.target.closest ? evt.target.closest('[data-tooltip]') : null;
        if (!leaving || leaving !== activeTarget) return;
        const entering = evt.relatedTarget && evt.relatedTarget.closest ? evt.relatedTarget.closest('[data-tooltip]') : null;
        if (entering === activeTarget) return;
        hideTooltip();
      });

      document.addEventListener('scroll', hideTooltip, true);
      window.addEventListener('blur', hideTooltip);
      window.addEventListener('resize', hideTooltip);
    }

    initSchematicHoverTooltips();

  </script>
{% endblock %}
